### USUÁRIO

Retorno do modelo ia:
 "Ajustando valores e implementações 
Para manter as arrays estáveis, não vamos reordená-las mais, removendo a ordenação de operações tanto no plano de execução quanto na compressão. A separação de domínios para os hashes (como winner_pipeline_hash, search_space_id, etc.) será feito com SHA256("TEIA/<DOMÍNIO>/vX" || canon(obj)). Também vamos ajustar os exemplos e o código principal para refletir esses requisitos.

Implementando validação de JSON
Para validar a integridade dos dados, vamos restaurar, recanonizar e comparar bytes. No PowerShell, vamos ler o arquivo original como string, gerar a versão canonizada e comparar o hash SHA256 dos dados. Se houver discrepâncias, a validação será rejeitada. Implementaremos uma comparação personalizada com ordenação binária ordinal.

Ordenação ordinal em PowerShell
O PowerShell oferece a funcionalidade -CaseSensitive e permite definir um scriptblock para propriedades com o comando Sort-Object. No entanto, para uma ordenação ordinal, precisarei converter as strings para um array de bytes UTF-8 e compará-los lexicograficamente, respeitando a ordem dos caracteres ASCII.

Atualizando artefatos e comandos
Vamos remover a ordenação de operações no script PowerShell e implementar validação de canonicalização. Quando recuperar ou verificar dados, vamos verificar a igualdade dos bytes do arquivo com a versão canonizada. Também vamos separar domínios ao gerar provas e adicionar novos comandos, como 'prove', 'seed.canon' e 'proof.canon'. A atualização deve ser feita para v0.1.3, incluindo os ajustes para testes e novos requisitos.

Pensado para 38s
Feito
Análise pausada
Mostrar sempre detalhes
# Build Purificação v0.1.3–v0.2.2 pre-hotfix artifacts with canonicalizer v1 and domain-separated hashes
import os, json, hashlib, platform, sys, time

def sha256(b: bytes) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha256(b).hexdigest().upper()

def canon_dumps(obj) -> bytes:
    # Canonical JSON: sorted keys (binary ordinal), UTF-8 no BOM, LF, no spaces.
    # Python's sort_keys uses Unicode codepoint which aligns with ASCII ordinal for our keys.
    txt = json.dumps(obj, sort_keys=True, separators=(',',':'), ensure_ascii=False)
    if not txt.endswith("\n"):
        txt += "\n"
    # enforce LF
    txt = txt.replace("\r\n","\n").replace("\r","\n")
    return txt.encode("utf-8")

def ds_hash(domain: str, ver: str, obj) -> str:
    prefix = ("TEIA/"+domain+"/v"+ver).encode("ascii")
    body = canon_dumps(obj)
    return sha256(prefix + body)

outdir = "/mnt/data/mvp_core_v0_1_3"
os.makedirs(outdir, exist_ok=True)

# Budget B0 (canonical doc) with domain-separated hash for proof
budget_spec = {
  "id":"B0",
  "time_ms_max":1000,
  "memory_mb_max":256,
  "search_width":8,
  "tie_breakers":["seed_len","time_ms","mem_mb","ops_count"]
}
budget_bytes = canon_dumps(budget_spec)
budget_sha = ds_hash("BUDGET","1", budget_spec)
budget_path = os.path.join(outdir,"budget_B0.json")
with open(budget_path,"wb") as f: f.write(budget_bytes)

# Core script v0.1.3 (no plan.ops reordering, canonicalization validation, domain-sep helpers, new commands)
core_ps = r'''# TEIA Deterministic Symbolic Core — Canonizador v1 (v0.1.3)
# Invariants: deterministic, idempotent, canonical JSON only (seeds/proofs), no regime anywhere.
param(
  [Parameter(Position=0,Mandatory=$true)]
  [ValidateSet('core-id','restore','verify','compress','seed.canon','proof.canon','seed.diff','prove','budget.show')]
  [string]$cmd,
  [string]$seed,
  [string]$in,
  [string]$out,
  [ValidateSet('B0')]
  [string]$budget='B0'
)
$ErrorActionPreference='Stop'

# ---------- Binary ordinal canonical JSON ----------
function Escape-Json([string]$s){
  $sb=New-Object System.Text.StringBuilder
  foreach($ch in $s.ToCharArray()){
    $code=[int][char]$ch
    switch($code){
      0x22 { [void]$sb.Append('\\"'); continue }
      0x5C { [void]$sb.Append('\\\\'); continue }
      0x08 { [void]$sb.Append('\\b'); continue }
      0x0C { [void]$sb.Append('\\f'); continue }
      0x0A { [void]$sb.Append('\\n'); continue }
      0x0D { [void]$sb.Append('\\r'); continue }
      0x09 { [void]$sb.Append('\\t'); continue }
    }
    if($code -lt 0x20){ [void]$sb.Append(('\\u{0:X4}' -f $code)) } else { [void]$sb.Append($ch) }
  }
  $sb.ToString()
}

function Ordinal-Key([string]$k){
  $bytes=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetBytes($k)
  # Represent as hex string to preserve bytewise order in Sort-Object
  return ([System.BitConverter]::ToString($bytes)).Replace('-','')
}

function To-CanonicalJson([object]$obj){
  if($null -eq $obj){ return 'null' }
  if($obj -is [string]){ return '"' + (Escape-Json $obj) + '"' }
  if($obj -is [bool]){ return ($obj.ToString().ToLower()) }
  if($obj -is [System.IFormattable]){ return ([System.Convert]::ToString($obj,[System.Globalization.CultureInfo]::InvariantCulture)) }
  if($obj -is [System.Collections.IDictionary]){
    $pairs=@()
    $keys=@($obj.Keys) | Sort-Object -Property @{Expression={ Ordinal-Key $_ }}, @{Expression={ $_ } }
    foreach($k in $keys){ $v=$obj[$k]; $pairs+=('"' + (Escape-Json [string]$k) + '":' + (To-CanonicalJson $v)) }
    return '{' + ($pairs -join ',') + '}'
  }
  if($obj -is [System.Collections.IEnumerable] -and -not ($obj -is [string])){
    $parts=@()
    foreach($x in $obj){ $parts+=(To-CanonicalJson $x) } # arrays are kept in original order
    return '[' + ($parts -join ',') + ']'
  }
  return ('"' + (Escape-Json ($obj.ToString())) + '"')
}

function Write-CanonicalJson([object]$obj,[string]$dest){
  $json=(To-CanonicalJson $obj) + "`n"
  $enc=New-Object System.Text.UTF8Encoding($false)
  [System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($dest,$json,$enc)
}

function CanonicalBytes([object]$obj){
  $json=(To-CanonicalJson $obj) + "`n"
  return [System.Text.UTF8Encoding]::new($false).GetBytes($json)
}

# ---------- Hashing ----------
function Get-CoreId {
  $bytes=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($PSCommandPath)
  $sha=[System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create()
  $hash=$sha.ComputeHash($bytes)
  ($hash|ForEach-Object{$_.ToString('X2')}) -join ''
}

function DS-Hash([string]$domain,[string]$v,[object]$obj){
  $prefix=[System.Text.Encoding]::ASCII.GetBytes("TEIA/$domain/v$($v)")
  $body=(CanonicalBytes $obj)
  $sha=[System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create()
  $h=$sha.ComputeHash( $prefix + $body )
  ($h|ForEach-Object{$_.ToString('X2')}) -join ''
}

# ---------- JSON IO ----------
function Read-Json([string]$path){
  $rawBytes=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($path)
  if($rawBytes.Length -ge 3 -and $rawBytes[0] -eq 0xEF -and $rawBytes[1] -eq 0xBB -and $rawBytes[2] -eq 0xBF){ throw "BOM not allowed" }
  foreach($b in $rawBytes){ if($b -eq 0x0D){ throw "CR not allowed; must use LF only" } }
  $raw=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetString($rawBytes)
  try { $obj=($raw | ConvertFrom-Json -AsHashtable) } catch { throw "Invalid JSON" }
  # Canonicalization check
  $canon = ([System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetString( (CanonicalBytes $obj) ))
  if($raw -ne $canon){ throw "Non-canonical JSON: recanonicalization differs bytewise" }
  return $obj
}

# ---------- DSL ops (no reordering) ----------
function Hex-To-Bytes([string]$hex){
  $clean=($hex -replace '\s','')
  if(($clean.Length%2)-ne 0){ throw "write.hex: hex length must be even" }
  $arr=New-Object byte[] ($clean.Length/2)
  for($i=0;$i -lt $arr.Length;$i++){ $arr[$i]=[Convert]::ToByte($clean.Substring($i*2,2),16) }
  return $arr
}

function Execute-Plan($plan){
  $ops=$plan.ops
  if(-not $ops){ return ,@() }
  $buf=New-Object System.Collections.Generic.List[byte]
  foreach($op in $ops){
    $name=$op.op; $args=$op.args
    switch($name){
      'gen.repeat' {
        if(-not $args.ContainsKey('byte') -or -not $args.ContainsKey('count')){ throw "gen.repeat requires args.byte and args.count" }
        $b=[byte]$args.byte; $count=[uint64]$args.count
        $chunk=New-Object byte[] ([Math]::Min(1048576,[int][Math]::Max(1,[int]$count)))
        for($i=0;$i -lt $chunk.Length;$i++){ $chunk[$i]=$b }
        $remaining=$count
        while($remaining -gt 0){ $take=[int]([Math]::Min($remaining,[uint64]$chunk.Length)); $buf.AddRange($chunk[0..($take-1)]); $remaining-=[uint64]$take }
      }
      'write.hex' { if(-not $args.ContainsKey('data')){ throw "write.hex requires args.data" }; $bytes=Hex-To-Bytes $args.data; $buf.AddRange($bytes) }
      default { throw "Unsupported op: $name" }
    }
  }
  return ,$buf.ToArray()
}

# ---------- Commands ----------
function Do-Restore([string]$seedPath,[string]$outPath){
  if(-not $seedPath){ throw "restore: --seed <path> is required" }
  if(-not $outPath){ throw "restore: --out <path> is required" }
  $s=Read-Json $seedPath
  if($s.ContainsKey('core_sha256')){ $s.core_sha256=$s.core_sha256.ToUpper() }
  if($s.ContainsKey('output_sha256')){ $s.output_sha256=$s.output_sha256.ToUpper() }
  $coreId=Get-CoreId
  if($coreId -ne $s.core_sha256){ throw "core hash mismatch: seed=$($s.core_sha256) core=$coreId" }
  $bytes=Execute-Plan $s.plan; if($null -eq $bytes){ $bytes=@() }
  if([uint64]$s.output_size -ne [uint64]$bytes.Length){ throw "size mismatch: expected $($s.output_size) got $($bytes.Length)" }
  $dir=Split-Path -Parent $outPath; if(-not (Test-Path -LiteralPath $dir)){ New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $dir -Force|Out-Null }
  [System.IO.File]::WriteAllBytes($outPath,$bytes)
  $h=Get-FileHash -LiteralPath $outPath -Algorithm SHA256
  if($h.Hash.ToUpper() -ne $s.output_sha256){ throw "sha256 mismatch: expected $($s.output_sha256) got $($h.Hash.ToUpper())" }
  Write-Host "OK restore | out=$outPath | size=$($bytes.Length) | sha256=$($h.Hash.ToUpper())"
}

function Do-Verify([string]$seedPath,[string]$filePath){
  if(-not $seedPath){ throw "verify: --seed <path> required" }
  if(-not $filePath){ throw "verify: --file <path> required" }
  $s=Read-Json $seedPath
  $h=Get-FileHash -LiteralPath $filePath -Algorithm SHA256
  if($h.Hash.ToUpper() -ne $s.output_sha256.ToUpper()){ throw "verify failed: file sha256=$($h.Hash.ToUpper()) != seed sha256=$($s.output_sha256.ToUpper())" }
  if((Get-Item $filePath).Length -ne [int64]$s.output_size){ throw "verify failed: size mismatch" }
  Write-Host "OK verify | file=$filePath"
}

function Do-Compress([string]$inPath,[string]$seedOut){
  if(-not $inPath){ throw "compress: --in <path> required" }
  if(-not $seedOut){ throw "compress: --out <seed> required" }
  $max=10485760
  $fi=Get-Item -LiteralPath $inPath
  if($fi.Length -gt $max){ throw "MVP compress supports files <= 10MiB" }
  $bytes=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($inPath)
  $coreId=Get-CoreId
  $shaOut=(Get-FileHash -LiteralPath $inPath -Algorithm SHA256).Hash.ToUpper()
  $b0=$bytes[0]; $allSame=$true
  for($i=1;$i -lt $bytes.Length;$i++){ if($bytes[$i] -ne $b0){ $allSame=$false; break } }
  if($allSame){
    $ops=@(@{ op="gen.repeat"; args=@{ byte=[int]$b0; count=[uint64]$bytes.Length } })
  } elseif($bytes.Length -le 4096){
    $hex=-join ($bytes|ForEach-Object{ $_.ToString('X2') })
    $ops=@(@{ op="write.hex"; args=@{ data=$hex } })
  } else { throw "MVP compress: unsupported pattern" }
  $seedObj=[ordered]@{
    budget_id     = $budget
    core_sha256   = $coreId
    core_version  = "v0.1.3"
    output_sha256 = $shaOut
    output_size   = [uint64]$bytes.Length
    plan          = [ordered]@{
      dsl_version = "v0.1.3"
      ops         = $ops  # arrays stay in provided order
    }
  }
  Write-CanonicalJson $seedObj $seedOut
  Write-Host "OK compress | seed=$seedOut"
}

function Do-Canon([string]$inPath,[string]$outPath){
  $obj = (Read-Json $inPath) # Read-Json already enforces canonical; just re-emit
  Write-CanonicalJson $obj $outPath
  Write-Host "OK canon | out=$outPath"
}

function Do-SeedDiff([string]$a,[string]$b){
  $oa=Read-Json $a; $ob=Read-Json $b
  $ba=CanonicalBytes $oa; $bb=CanonicalBytes $ob
  $ha=([System.BitConverter]::ToString(( [System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create().ComputeHash($ba) ))).Replace('-','')
  $hb=([System.BitConverter]::ToString(( [System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create().ComputeHash($bb) ))).Replace('-','')
  if($ha -eq $hb){ Write-Host "EQUAL" } else { Write-Host "DIFF `nA=$ha`nB=$hb" }
}

function Do-Prove([string]$seedPath,[string]$outPath){
  $s=Read-Json $seedPath
  $coreId=Get-CoreId
  if($coreId -ne $s.core_sha256){ throw "core hash mismatch" }
  $seedCanon = (CanonicalBytes $s)
  $seedSha = ([System.BitConverter]::ToString(( [System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create().ComputeHash($seedCanon) ))).Replace('-','')
  # Budget content (B0)
  $budgetObj = @{ id="B0"; time_ms_max=1000; memory_mb_max=256; search_width=8; tie_breakers=@("seed_len","time_ms","mem_mb","ops_count") }
  $searchSpace = @{ ops=@("gen.repeat","write.hex") }
  $scheduler   = @{ scheduler="lexicographic-v1" }
  $search_space_id = (DS-Hash "BUDGET" "1" $searchSpace) # domain separation example (use BUDGET for space too? we keep as BUDGET-like domain)
  $scheduler_id    = (DS-Hash "SCHED" "1" $scheduler)
  $budget_sha      = (DS-Hash "BUDGET" "1" $budgetObj)
  $winner_pipeline_hash = (DS-Hash "PLAN" "1" $s.plan)
  $proof = [ordered]@{
    budget_id = "B0"
    core_sha256 = $coreId
    core_version = $s.core_version
    dsl_version = $s.plan.dsl_version
    ops_count = $s.plan.ops.Count
    output_sha256 = $s.output_sha256
    output_size = [uint64]$s.output_size
    seed_sha256 = $seedSha
    decision_trace = [ordered]@{
      search_space_id = $search_space_id
      scheduler_id = $scheduler_id
      candidates_evaluated = 1
      ranking_topk = @(@{ pipeline_hash = $winner_pipeline_hash; cost = 0 })
      winner_pipeline_hash = $winner_pipeline_hash
      env_fingerprint = [ordered]@{
        os = $PSVersionTable.OS
        ps = $PSVersionTable.PSVersion.ToString()
        locale = "C"
        arch = $env:PROCESSOR_ARCHITECTURE
      }
      budget_spec_sha256 = $budget_sha
    }
    created_utc = (Get-Date).ToUniversalTime().ToString("o")
  }
  Write-CanonicalJson $proof $outPath
  Write-Host "OK prove | out=$outPath"
}

function Show-Budget(){
  $obj = @{ id="B0"; time_ms_max=1000; memory_mb_max=256; search_width=8; tie_breakers=@("seed_len","time_ms","mem_mb","ops_count") }
  $obj
}

switch($cmd){
  'core-id'    { Write-Host (Get-CoreId); break }
  'restore'    { Do-Restore -seedPath $seed -outPath $out; break }
  'verify'     { Do-Verify  -seedPath $seed -filePath $in; break }
  'compress'   { Do-Compress -inPath $in -seedOut $out; break }
  'seed.canon' { Do-Canon -inPath $in -outPath $out; break }
  'proof.canon'{ Do-Canon -inPath $in -outPath $out; break }
  'seed.diff'  { Do-SeedDiff -a $in -b $out; break }
  'prove'      { Do-Prove -seedPath $seed -outPath $out; break }
  'budget.show'{ Show-Budget | Out-String | Write-Host; break }
}
'''
core_path = os.path.join(outdir,"TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1")
with open(core_path,"w",encoding="utf-8",newline="\n") as f: f.write(core_ps)
core_sha = sha256(open(core_path,"rb").read())

  "output_sha256": output_sha,
  "output_size": count,

  "description":"Canonical JSON (binary ordinal keys, UTF-8 no BOM, LF). Arrays preserve order. No regime. HEX UPPERCASE. Integers are non-negative 64-bit.",
  "type":"object",

    "core_sha256":{"type":"string","pattern":"^[A-F0-9]{64}$"},

# BNF (arrays preserve order)
bnf_txt = """TEIA-DSL v0.1.3 (BNF mínima, canônica)
<seed> ::= '{' <pairs> '}'
<pairs> ::= <pair> | <pair> ',' <pairs>
<pair> ::= '"budget_id":' <string>
         | '"core_sha256":' <hex64>
         | '"core_version":' <string>
         | '"output_sha256":' <hex64>
         | '"output_size":' <uint64>
         | '"plan":' <plan>
<plan> ::= '{' '"dsl_version":' <string> ',' '"ops":' '[' <ops> ']' '}'
<ops> ::= <op> | <op> ',' <ops>
<op>  ::= '{' '"args":' <object> ',' '"op":' <enum_op> '}'   ; arrays preservam ordem de chegada
<enum_op> ::= '"gen.repeat"' | '"write.hex"'
<hex64> ::= '"' 64*<HEX> '"'
<HEX> ::= '0'..'9' | 'A'..'F'
<string> ::= JSON string
<uint64> ::= JSON integer 0..18446744073709551615
<object> ::= JSON object (chaves ordenadas por ordem binária)
"""
bnf_bytes = canon_dumps({"bnf":bnf_txt})
bnf_sha = sha256(bnf_bytes)
bnf_path = os.path.join(outdir,"dsl_min_bnf.txt")
with open(bnf_path,"wb") as f: f.write(bnf_bytes)

# Retry: generate the artifacts again (smaller chunks writing) to avoid transient issues
import os, json, hashlib, platform, time

def sha256(b: bytes) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha256(b).hexdigest().upper()

def canon_dumps(obj) -> bytes:
    txt = json.dumps(obj, sort_keys=True, separators=(',',':'), ensure_ascii=False)
    txt = txt.replace("\r\n","\n").replace("\r","\n")
    if not txt.endswith("\n"):
        txt += "\n"
    return txt.encode("utf-8")

def ds_hash(domain: str, ver: str, obj) -> str:
    prefix = ("TEIA/"+domain+"/v"+ver).encode("ascii")
    body = canon_dumps(obj)
    return sha256(prefix + body)

outdir = "/mnt/data/mvp_core_v0_1_3"
os.makedirs(outdir, exist_ok=True)

# 1) Budget
budget_spec = {"id":"B0","time_ms_max":1000,"memory_mb_max":256,"search_width":8,"tie_breakers":["seed_len","time_ms","mem_mb","ops_count"]}
budget_bytes = canon_dumps(budget_spec)
budget_sha = ds_hash("BUDGET","1", budget_spec)
with open(os.path.join(outdir,"budget_B0.json"),"wb") as f: f.write(budget_bytes)

# 2) Core PS1
core_ps = r'''# TEIA Deterministic Symbolic Core — Canonizador v1 (v0.1.3)
param(
  [Parameter(Position=0,Mandatory=$true)]
  [ValidateSet('core-id','restore','verify','compress','seed.canon','proof.canon','seed.diff','prove','budget.show')]
  [string]$cmd,[string]$seed,[string]$in,[string]$out,[ValidateSet('B0')][string]$budget='B0'
)
$ErrorActionPreference='Stop'
function Escape-Json([string]$s){ $sb=New-Object System.Text.StringBuilder; foreach($ch in $s.ToCharArray()){ $code=[int][char]$ch; switch($code){ 0x22{[void]$sb.Append('\\"');continue};0x5C{[void]$sb.Append('\\\\');continue};0x08{[void]$sb.Append('\\b');continue};0x0C{[void]$sb.Append('\\f');continue};0x0A{[void]$sb.Append('\\n');continue};0x0D{[void]$sb.Append('\\r');continue};0x09{[void]$sb.Append('\\t');continue} } if($code -lt 0x20){[void]$sb.Append(('\\u{0:X4}'-f $code))}else{[void]$sb.Append($ch)} } $sb.ToString() }
function Ordinal-Key([string]$k){ $bytes=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetBytes($k); ([System.BitConverter]::ToString($bytes)).Replace('-','') }
function To-CanonicalJson([object]$obj){
  if($null -eq $obj){return 'null'}
  if($obj -is [string]){return '"' + (Escape-Json $obj) + '"'}
  if($obj -is [bool]){return ($obj.ToString().ToLower())}
  if($obj -is [System.IFormattable]){return ([System.Convert]::ToString($obj,[System.Globalization.CultureInfo]::InvariantCulture))}
  if($obj -is [System.Collections.IDictionary]){ $pairs=@(); $keys=@($obj.Keys)|Sort-Object -Property @{Expression={ Ordinal-Key $_ }}, @{Expression={ $_ }}; foreach($k in $keys){ $v=$obj[$k]; $pairs+=('"' + (Escape-Json [string]$k) + '":' + (To-CanonicalJson $v)) } return '{' + ($pairs -join ',') + '}' }
  if($obj -is [System.Collections.IEnumerable] -and -not ($obj -is [string])){ $parts=@(); foreach($x in $obj){ $parts+=(To-CanonicalJson $x) } return '[' + ($parts -join ',') + ']' }
  return ('"' + (Escape-Json ($obj.ToString())) + '"')
}
function Write-CanonicalJson([object]$obj,[string]$dest){ $json=(To-CanonicalJson $obj) + "`n"; $enc=New-Object System.Text.UTF8Encoding($false); [System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($dest,$json,$enc) }
function CanonicalBytes([object]$obj){ $json=(To-CanonicalJson $obj) + "`n"; [System.Text.UTF8Encoding]::new($false).GetBytes($json) }
function Get-CoreId{ $bytes=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($PSCommandPath); $sha=[System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create(); $hash=$sha.ComputeHash($bytes); ($hash|ForEach-Object{$_.ToString('X2')}) -join '' }
function DS-Hash([string]$domain,[string]$v,[object]$obj){ $prefix=[System.Text.Encoding]::ASCII.GetBytes("TEIA/$domain/v$($v)"); $body=(CanonicalBytes $obj); $sha=[System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create(); $h=$sha.ComputeHash($prefix+$body); ($h|ForEach-Object{$_.ToString('X2')}) -join '' }
function Read-Json([string]$path){ $rawBytes=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($path); if($rawBytes.Length -ge 3 -and $rawBytes[0]-eq 0xEF -and $rawBytes[1]-eq 0xBB -and $rawBytes[2]-eq 0xBF){throw "BOM not allowed"}; foreach($b in $rawBytes){ if($b -eq 0x0D){ throw "CR not allowed; must use LF only" } } $raw=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetString($rawBytes); try{ $obj=($raw|ConvertFrom-Json -AsHashtable) }catch{ throw "Invalid JSON" } $canon=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetString((CanonicalBytes $obj)); if($raw -ne $canon){ throw "Non-canonical JSON: recanonicalization differs bytewise" } $obj }
function Hex-To-Bytes([string]$hex){ $clean=($hex -replace '\s',''); if(($clean.Length%2)-ne 0){ throw "write.hex: hex length must be even" } $arr=New-Object byte[] ($clean.Length/2); for($i=0;$i -lt $arr.Length;$i++){ $arr[$i]=[Convert]::ToByte($clean.Substring($i*2,2),16) } $arr }
function Execute-Plan($plan){ $ops=$plan.ops; if(-not $ops){return ,@()} $buf=New-Object System.Collections.Generic.List[byte]; foreach($op in $ops){ $name=$op.op; $args=$op.args; switch($name){ 'gen.repeat' { if(-not $args.ContainsKey('byte') -or -not $args.ContainsKey('count')){ throw "gen.repeat requires args.byte and args.count" } $b=[byte]$args.byte; $count=[uint64]$args.count; $chunk=New-Object byte[] ([Math]::Min(1048576,[int][Math]::Max(1,[int]$count))); for($i=0;$i -lt $chunk.Length;$i++){ $chunk[$i]=$b } $remaining=$count; while($remaining -gt 0){ $take=[int]([Math]::Min($remaining,[uint64]$chunk.Length)); $buf.AddRange($chunk[0..($take-1)]); $remaining-=[uint64]$take } } 'write.hex' { if(-not $args.ContainsKey('data')){ throw "write.hex requires args.data" } $bytes=Hex-To-Bytes $args.data; $buf.AddRange($bytes) } default { throw "Unsupported op: $name" } } } ,$buf.ToArray() }
function Do-Restore([string]$seedPath,[string]$outPath){ if(-not $seedPath){ throw "restore: --seed <path> is required" } if(-not $outPath){ throw "restore: --out <path> is required" } $s=Read-Json $seedPath; if($s.ContainsKey('core_sha256')){ $s.core_sha256=$s.core_sha256.ToUpper() } if($s.ContainsKey('output_sha256')){ $s.output_sha256=$s.output_sha256.ToUpper() } $coreId=Get-CoreId; if($coreId -ne $s.core_sha256){ throw "core hash mismatch: seed=$($s.core_sha256) core=$coreId" } $bytes=Execute-Plan $s.plan; if($null -eq $bytes){ $bytes=@() } if([uint64]$s.output_size -ne [uint64]$bytes.Length){ throw "size mismatch: expected $($s.output_size) got $($bytes.Length)" } $dir=Split-Path -Parent $outPath; if(-not (Test-Path -LiteralPath $dir)){ New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $dir -Force|Out-Null } [System.IO.File]::WriteAllBytes($outPath,$bytes); $h=Get-FileHash -LiteralPath $outPath -Algorithm SHA256; if($h.Hash.ToUpper() -ne $s.output_sha256){ throw "sha256 mismatch: expected $($s.output_sha256) got $($h.Hash.ToUpper())" } Write-Host "OK restore | out=$outPath | size=$($bytes.Length) | sha256=$($h.Hash.ToUpper())" }
function Do-Verify([string]$seedPath,[string]$filePath){ if(-not $seedPath){ throw "verify: --seed <path> required" } if(-not $filePath){ throw "verify: --file <path> required" } $s=Read-Json $seedPath; $h=Get-FileHash -LiteralPath $filePath -Algorithm SHA256; if($h.Hash.ToUpper() -ne $s.output_sha256.ToUpper()){ throw "verify failed: file sha256=$($h.Hash.ToUpper()) != seed sha256=$($s.output_sha256.ToUpper())" } if((Get-Item $filePath).Length -ne [int64]$s.output_size){ throw "verify failed: size mismatch" } Write-Host "OK verify | file=$filePath" }
function Do-Compress([string]$inPath,[string]$seedOut){ if(-not $inPath){ throw "compress: --in <path> required" } if(-not $seedOut){ throw "compress: --out <seed> required" } $max=10485760; $fi=Get-Item -LiteralPath $inPath; if($fi.Length -gt $max){ throw "MVP compress supports files <= 10MiB" } $bytes=[System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($inPath); $coreId=Get-CoreId; $shaOut=(Get-FileHash -LiteralPath $inPath -Algorithm SHA256).Hash.ToUpper(); $b0=$bytes[0]; $allSame=$true; for($i=1;$i -lt $bytes.Length;$i++){ if($bytes[$i] -ne $b0){ $allSame=$false; break } } if($allSame){ $ops=@(@{ op="gen.repeat"; args=@{ byte=[int]$b0; count=[uint64]$bytes.Length } }) } elseif($bytes.Length -le 4096){ $hex=-join ($bytes|ForEach-Object{ $_.ToString('X2') }); $ops=@(@{ op="write.hex"; args=@{ data=$hex } }) } else { throw "MVP compress: unsupported pattern" } $seedObj=[ordered]@{ budget_id=$budget; core_sha256=$coreId; core_version="v0.1.3"; output_sha256=$shaOut; output_size=[uint64]$bytes.Length; plan=[ordered]@{ dsl_version="v0.1.3"; ops=$ops } }; Write-CanonicalJson $seedObj $seedOut; Write-Host "OK compress | seed=$seedOut" }
function Do-Canon([string]$inPath,[string]$outPath){ $obj=(Read-Json $inPath); Write-CanonicalJson $obj $outPath; Write-Host "OK canon | out=$outPath" }
function Do-SeedDiff([string]$a,[string]$b){ $oa=Read-Json $a; $ob=Read-Json $b; $ba=CanonicalBytes $oa; $bb=CanonicalBytes $ob; $sha=[System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create(); $ha=([System.BitConverter]::ToString(($sha.ComputeHash($ba)))).Replace('-',''); $hb=([System.BitConverter]::ToString(($sha.ComputeHash($bb)))).Replace('-',''); if($ha -eq $hb){ Write-Host "EQUAL" } else { Write-Host "DIFF `nA=$ha`nB=$hb" } }
function Do-Prove([string]$seedPath,[string]$outPath){ $s=Read-Json $seedPath; $coreId=Get-CoreId; if($coreId -ne $s.core_sha256){ throw "core hash mismatch" } $seedCanon=(CanonicalBytes $s); $sha=[System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256]::Create(); $seedSha=([System.BitConverter]::ToString(($sha.ComputeHash($seedCanon)))).Replace('-',''); $budgetObj=@{ id="B0"; time_ms_max=1000; memory_mb_max=256; search_width=8; tie_breakers=@("seed_len","time_ms","mem_mb","ops_count") }; $searchSpace=@{ ops=@("gen.repeat","write.hex") }; $scheduler=@{ scheduler="lexicographic-v1" }; $search_space_id=(DS-Hash "SPACE" "1" $searchSpace); $scheduler_id=(DS-Hash "SCHED" "1" $scheduler); $budget_sha=(DS-Hash "BUDGET" "1" $budgetObj); $winner_pipeline_hash=(DS-Hash "PLAN" "1" $s.plan); $proof=[ordered]@{ budget_id="B0"; core_sha256=$coreId; core_version=$s.core_version; dsl_version=$s.plan.dsl_version; ops_count=$s.plan.ops.Count; output_sha256=$s.output_sha256; output_size=[uint64]$s.output_size; seed_sha256=$seedSha; decision_trace=[ordered]@{ search_space_id=$search_space_id; scheduler_id=$scheduler_id; candidates_evaluated=1; ranking_topk=@(@{ pipeline_hash=$winner_pipeline_hash; cost=0 }); winner_pipeline_hash=$winner_pipeline_hash; env_fingerprint=[ordered]@{ os=$PSVersionTable.OS; ps=$PSVersionTable.PSVersion.ToString(); locale="C"; arch=$env:PROCESSOR_ARCHITECTURE }; budget_spec_sha256=$budget_sha }; created_utc=(Get-Date).ToUniversalTime().ToString("o") }; Write-CanonicalJson $proof $outPath; Write-Host "OK prove | out=$outPath" }
function Show-Budget(){ $obj=@{ id="B0"; time_ms_max=1000; memory_mb_max=256; search_width=8; tie_breakers=@("seed_len","time_ms","mem_mb","ops_count") }; $obj }
switch($cmd){
  'core-id'    { Write-Host (Get-CoreId); break }
  'restore'    { Do-Restore -seedPath $seed -outPath $out; break }
  'verify'     { Do-Verify  -seedPath $seed -filePath $in; break }
  'compress'   { Do-Compress -inPath $in -seedOut $out; break }
  'seed.canon' { Do-Canon -inPath $in -outPath $out; break }
  'proof.canon'{ Do-Canon -inPath $in -outPath $out; break }
  'seed.diff'  { Do-SeedDiff -a $in -b $out; break }
  'prove'      { Do-Prove -seedPath $seed -outPath $out; break }
  'budget.show'{ Show-Budget | Out-String | Write-Host; break }
}
'''
core_path = os.path.join(outdir,"TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1")
with open(core_path,"w",encoding="utf-8",newline="\n") as f: f.write(core_ps)
core_sha = sha256(open(core_path,"rb").read())

# 3) Seed example
byte_val = 0x41
count = 1024*1024
output_sha = sha256(bytes([byte_val])*count)
seed_obj = {
  "budget_id":"B0",
  "core_sha256": core_sha,
  "core_version":"v0.1.3",
  "output_sha256": output_sha,
  "output_size": count,
  "plan": {"dsl_version":"v0.1.3","ops":[{"op":"gen.repeat","args":{"byte":byte_val,"count":count}}]}
}
seed_bytes = canon_dumps(seed_obj)
seed_sha = sha256(seed_bytes)
seed_path = os.path.join(outdir,"example_seed_repeatA.json")
with open(seed_path,"wb") as f: f.write(seed_bytes)

# 4) Proof example
decision_trace = {
  "search_space_id": ds_hash("SPACE","1", {"ops":["gen.repeat","write.hex"]}),
  "scheduler_id": ds_hash("SCHED","1", {"scheduler":"lexicographic-v1"}),
  "candidates_evaluated": 1,
  "ranking_topk":[ {"pipeline_hash": ds_hash("PLAN","1", seed_obj["plan"]), "cost": 0} ],
  "winner_pipeline_hash": ds_hash("PLAN","1", seed_obj["plan"]),
  "env_fingerprint": {"os": platform.system(),"python": platform.python_version(),"locale":"C","arch": platform.machine()},
  "budget_spec_sha256": budget_sha
}
proof_obj = {
  "budget_id":"B0",
  "core_sha256": core_sha,
  "core_version":"v0.1.3",
  "dsl_version":"v0.1.3",
  "ops_count": 1,
  "output_sha256": output_sha,
  "output_size": count,
  "seed_sha256": seed_sha,
  "decision_trace": decision_trace,
  "created_utc": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
}
proof_bytes = canon_dumps(proof_obj)
proof_sha = sha256(proof_bytes)
proof_path = os.path.join(outdir,"example_proof.json")
with open(proof_path,"wb") as f: f.write(proof_bytes)

# 5) Schema & BNF
schema = {
  "$schema":"https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id":"https://teia/aion/seed_schema_v1.json",
  "title":"TEIA Seed Schema v1 (Purificação 0.1.3)",
  "description":"Canonical JSON (binary ordinal keys, UTF-8 no BOM, LF). Arrays preserve order. No regime. HEX UPPERCASE. Integers are non-negative 64-bit.",
  "type":"object",
  "required":["core_sha256","core_version","budget_id","output_size","output_sha256","plan"],
  "properties":{
    "budget_id":{"type":"string","enum":["B0"]},
    "core_sha256":{"type":"string","pattern":"^[A-F0-9]{64}$"},
    "core_version":{"type":"string"},
    "output_sha256":{"type":"string","pattern":"^[A-F0-9]{64}$"},
    "output_size":{"type":"integer","minimum":0,"maximum":18446744073709551615},
    "plan":{
      "type":"object",
      "required":["dsl_version","ops"],
      "properties":{
        "dsl_version":{"type":"string"},
        "ops":{
          "type":"array",
          "items":{
            "type":"object",
            "required":["op","args"],
            "properties":{
              "op":{"type":"string","enum":["gen.repeat","write.hex"]},
              "args":{"type":"object"}
            },
            "additionalProperties":False
          }
        }
      },
      "additionalProperties":False
    }
  },
  "additionalProperties":False
}
schema_bytes = canon_dumps(schema)
schema_sha = sha256(schema_bytes)
schema_path = os.path.join(outdir,"seed_schema_v1.json")
with open(schema_path,"wb") as f: f.write(schema_bytes)

bnf_txt = """TEIA-DSL v0.1.3 (BNF mínima, canônica)
<seed> ::= '{' <pairs> '}'
<pairs> ::= <pair> | <pair> ',' <pairs>
<pair> ::= '"budget_id":' <string>
         | '"core_sha256":' <hex64>
         | '"core_version":' <string>
         | '"output_sha256":' <hex64>
         | '"output_size":' <uint64>
         | '"plan":' <plan>
<plan> ::= '{' '"dsl_version":' <string> ',' '"ops":' '[' <ops> ']' '}'
<ops> ::= <op> | <op> ',' <ops>
<op>  ::= '{' '"args":' <object> ',' '"op":' <enum_op> '}'   ; arrays preservam ordem
<enum_op> ::= '"gen.repeat"' | '"write.hex"'
<hex64> ::= '"' 64*<HEX> '"'
<HEX> ::= '0'..'9' | 'A'..'F'
<string> ::= JSON string
<uint64> ::= JSON integer 0..18446744073709551615
<object> ::= JSON object (chaves ordenadas por ordem binária)
"""
bnf_bytes = canon_dumps({"bnf":bnf_txt})
bnf_sha = sha256(bnf_bytes)
bnf_path = os.path.join(outdir,"dsl_min_bnf.txt")
with open(bnf_path,"wb") as f: f.write(bnf_bytes)

🔧 Resumo do delta aplicado (sobre v0.1.2)

Pré-hotfix imediato

Arrays ≠ dicionários: nunca reordenar plan.ops. (Removi a ordenação de ops no core.)

Ordenação de chaves: ordem binária (ordinal). Canonizador próprio garante chaves por bytes (0–9 < A–Z < a–z), sem influência de locale/cultura.

Validação de canonicidade na entrada: restore/verify/prove/seed.diff/seed.canon rejeitam seeds/proofs não-canônicas (o core recanoniza e compara byte a byte; divergência ⇒ erro).

Domain separation nos hashes: agora usamos SHA256("TEIA/<DOMÍNIO>/vX" || canon(obj)) para PLAN, SPACE (espaço de busca), SCHED (scheduler) e BUDGET.

Timestamps só no proof. Seed permanece atemporal.

“regime”: já estava purgado; mantido expurgo total (schema/BNF/exemplos/core).

Novos comandos/fluxos

prove gera proof canônico com decision_trace completo e hashes com domain separation.

budget.show exibe o documento canônico do orçamento (B0).

▶️ CLI (PowerShell 7+) — comandos principais
# ID do core (canônico, LF, UTF-8 sem BOM)
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 core-id

# Canonizar (e validar) uma seed; rejeita se não for canônica
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 seed.canon --in .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\seed_canon.json

# Diferença canônica entre duas seeds (igualdade = bytes idênticos)
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 seed.diff --in .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\seed_canon.json

# Restore (exige seed canônica; valida size+SHA; sem acesso ao original)
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 restore --seed .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\out.bin

# Verify (arquivo vs seed)
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 verify --seed .\example_seed_repeatA.json --in .\out.bin

# Provar (gera proof canônico com domain separation)
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 prove --seed .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\example_proof.json

# Mostrar orçamento canônico
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 budget.show

✅ Testes A–E (devem passar)

A) restore(seed) ⇒ SHA do restaurado == output_sha256

pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 restore --seed .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\out.bin


B) compress(restore(seed)) ⇒ seed' == seed (bytes canônicos)

pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 compress --in .\out.bin --out .\seed_prime.json
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 seed.diff --in .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\seed_prime.json
# Esperado: EQUAL


C) Reexecuções N≥3, hosts distintos ⇒ todos os hashes idênticos

Compare core-id, seed_sha256, out.bin (SHA-256) e example_proof.json (hash idêntico).

D) Restore(Restore(seed)) é no-op

pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 restore --seed .\example_seed_repeatA.json --out .\out2.bin
# SHA256(out.bin) == SHA256(out2.bin)


E) Proof reconstituível (domain separation)

Recompute localmente:

winner_pipeline_hash = SHA256("TEIA/PLAN/v1" || canon(plan))

budget_spec_sha256 = SHA256("TEIA/BUDGET/v1" || canon(budget_B0.json))

scheduler_id, search_space_id idem.
Devem coincidir com os campos do example_proof.json.

🔒 Garantia denotativa

O plano é a única autoridade; nenhuma semântica residual de “regime” permanece.
Seeds e proofs devem ser canônicos: chaves em ordem binária, UTF-8 sem BOM, LF, sem espaços supérfluos, inteiros decimais (u64), HEX MAIÚSCULO, e arrays preservam a ordem. Qualquer divergência é rejeitada pelo core.

v0.1.6: budget.show expõe o B0 canônico; scheduler lexicográfico está identificado (IDs com domain separation).

v0.1.7: posso estender agora com rle.det, map.tile/patch, lz.det (restrito) e ref.dict(id) (dicionários canônicos versionados).

Se quiser, já sigo para v0.1.7 adicionando rle.det + novos exemplos de seed e asserções no prove, mantendo todos os contratos acima."

  (`<uint64> ::= JSON integer 0..18446744073709551615`; `<HEX> ::= '0'..'9' | 'A'..'F'`). fileciteturn2file2
- Documente os **rótulos de domain-separation** usados nos hashes (e.g., `TEIA/PLAN/v1`, `TEIA/SPACE/v1`, `TEIA/SCHED/v1`, `TEIA/BUDGET/v1`) para alinhar versão dos domínios; o proof já carrega IDs, mas a convenção textual não está explícita no bundle. fileciteturn2file0 fileciteturn2file3

**Checks rápidos recomendados (sanidade do core):**
- Remoção total de qualquer `Sort-Object` sobre `plan.ops` (arrays **não** podem ser reordenadas).
- `restore/verify/prove/seed.canon/seed.diff` devem **rejeitar JSON não canônico** (re-canoniza e compara bytes).
- `prove` deve emitir `winner_pipeline_hash`/`search_space_id`/`scheduler_id`/`budget_spec_sha256` coerentes com a política de domain-separation (mesmo host ≡ mesmo valor).

Se você mover os artefatos legados para `legacy/` (ou apagar) e ajustar os detalhes da BNF, o conjunto v0.1.3 fica **inteiramente alinhado** ao núcleo ontoprocedural determinístico.

""Pensado por 27 segundos" 
Planeando a atualização dos artefatos
O usuário quer que removamos ou arquivemos os artefatos antigos conflitantes com a linha canônica, incluindo itens como "seed_schema" e menções ao "regime". Além disso, solicita correções em intervalos BNF, documentação de rótulos de separação de domínio e checagens de sanidade. No entanto, não podemos excluir diretamente, mas podemos fornecer artefatos atualizados e sugerir substituir ou arquivar versões antigas.

Atualizando artefatos e verificações
O usuário precisa de um script PowerShell para localizar artefatos antigos relacionados a "regime" e "created_utc", movê-los para um diretório de arquivo, e também para canonizar os outros artefatos. Além disso, precisamos corrigir o BNF, incluindo intervalos explícitos e documentação de separação de domínio. Também devemos confirmar saneamento de dados (e.g., remoção de usos de Sort-Object), prover testes de validação, e entregar a versão atualizada de todos os artefatos.

Fornecendo artefatos e scripts
O usuário solicita um "bundle manifest" com a lista de rótulos de separação de domínio usados (como TEIA/PLAN/v1 e TEIA/SPACE/v1) e sua correspondência com a função ds_hash. Também pedem a documentação "domain_separation.md" com exemplos e IDs. Além disso, precisamos de um script para migrar "default" para "B0" nos seeds.

Resolvendo requisitos de migração e atualização
O usuário quer que a ferramenta de canonicalização reescreva os artefatos para o formato canônico, removendo "regime" e "meta". No entanto, não podemos alterar a semântica, então uma ferramenta de arquivamento será criada para os artefatos conflitantes. Além disso, precisamos fornecer artefatos atualizados, incluindo documentação e validação das modificações.

# Create additional artifacts: domain_separation.md, README_CANON_LINE.txt,
# TEIA-Canon-Sweep.ps1, TEIA-Canon-Migrate.ps1, and update BNF/schema if needed.
import os, json, hashlib, textwrap, datetime, platform

def sha256_path(p):
    h = hashlib.sha256()
    with open(p, "rb") as f:
        h.update(f.read())
    return h.hexdigest().upper()

root = "/mnt/data/mvp_core_v0_1_3"
os.makedirs(root, exist_ok=True)

# Load proof to extract DS IDs for documentation
proof_path = os.path.join(root, "example_proof.json")
with open(proof_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    proof = json.load(f)

ds_doc = f"""# TEIA — Domain Separation (Purificação canônica)

Esta política fixa *prefixos de domínio* para todos os hashes derivados de estruturas canônicas:

- **PLAN**: `TEIA/PLAN/v1 || canon(plan)` → `winner_pipeline_hash`
- **SPACE**: `TEIA/SPACE/v1 || canon({{"ops":[...]}})` → `search_space_id`
- **SCHED**: `TEIA/SCHED/v1 || canon({{"scheduler":"..."}})` → `scheduler_id`
- **BUDGET**: `TEIA/BUDGET/v1 || canon(budget_doc)` → `budget_spec_sha256`

Propriedades:
- **Determinismo** e **idempotência**: mesma entrada canônica ⇒ mesmo hash, em qualquer host.
- **Isolamento semântico**: cada domínio é independente (sem colisões acidentais entre objetos distintos).

Exemplo (do `example_proof.json` deste bundle):
- `winner_pipeline_hash` = **{proof["decision_trace"]["winner_pipeline_hash"]}**
- `search_space_id`     = **{proof["decision_trace"]["search_space_id"]}**
- `scheduler_id`        = **{proof["decision_trace"]["scheduler_id"]}**
- `budget_spec_sha256`  = **{proof["decision_trace"]["budget_spec_sha256"]}**

**Observação:** todos os objetos JSON acima são serializados em **forma canônica** (chaves em ordem binária,
UTF-8 sem BOM, LF, sem espaços supérfluos, inteiros decimais, HEX maiúsculo) antes do cálculo do hash.
"""

ds_path = os.path.join(root, "domain_separation.md")
with open(ds_path, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline="\n") as f:
    f.write(ds_doc)
ds_sha = sha256_path(ds_path)

readme = """TEIA — Linha Canônica (Purificação)

- JSON canônico: chaves ordenadas por **ordem binária (ordinal)**; UTF-8 **sem BOM**; **LF**; **sem espaços**.
- **Arrays preservam ordem** (nunca reordenar `plan.ops`).
- HEX **maiúsculo**; inteiros decimais (u64).
- **Seed**: sem timestamps e sem “regime” (purga total). Igualdade = **bytes idênticos**.
- **Proof**: inclui `decision_trace` e usa **domain separation** nos hashes (PLAN/SPACE/SCHED/BUDGET).
- **Budget**: documento canônico versionado (B0,B1,...).

Ferramentas (PowerShell 7+):
- `core-id`, `restore`, `verify`, `compress` (MVP determinístico)
- `seed.canon`, `proof.canon` (validam e reemitem canônico)
- `seed.diff` (compara seeds por bytes canônicos)
- `prove` (emite proof canônico)
- `budget.show` (exibe orçamento canônico)

Política de rejeição: qualquer JSON não-canônico é **rejeitado** (`Non-canonical JSON: recanonicalization differs bytewise`)."""

readme_path = os.path.join(root, "README_CANON_LINE.txt")
with open(readme_path, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline="\n") as f:
    f.write(readme)
readme_sha = sha256_path(readme_path)

# TEIA-Canon-Sweep.ps1: varredura, detecção e arquivamento de artefatos legados
sweep_ps = r'''# TEIA-Canon-Sweep.ps1 — Varredura e arquivamento de artefatos legados (regime/meta/default/bad-hex)
param(
  [string[]]$roots = @(".")
)
$ErrorActionPreference='Stop'
$archive = Join-Path (Get-Location) "TEIA_legacy_archive"
if(-not (Test-Path -LiteralPath $archive)){ New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $archive | Out-Null }

function Is-Legacy-SeedOrProof([string]$path){
  if(-not (Test-Path -LiteralPath $path)){ return $false }
  try {
    $raw = Get-Content -LiteralPath $path -Raw -Encoding UTF8
    $obj = $raw | ConvertFrom-Json -AsHashtable
  } catch { return $false }
  # flags: regime/meta.created_utc/budget_id default/hex lowercase
  if($obj.ContainsKey('regime')){ return $true }
  if($obj.ContainsKey('meta')){
    $m = $obj['meta']
    if($m -and ($m -is [System.Collections.IDictionary]) -and $m.ContainsKey('created_utc')){ return $true }
  }
  if($obj.ContainsKey('budget_id') -and $obj['budget_id'] -eq 'default'){ return $true }
  foreach($k in @('core_sha256','output_sha256','seed_sha256')){
    if($obj.ContainsKey($k)){ $v=[string]$obj[$k]; if($v -match '[a-f]'){ return $true } }
  }
  return $false
}

$files = @()
foreach($root in $roots){
  if(-not (Test-Path -LiteralPath $root)){ continue }
  $files += Get-ChildItem -LiteralPath $root -Recurse -File -Include *.json,*.txt -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
}
$legacy = @()
foreach($f in $files){
  $p = $f.FullName
  if($p -match '(?i)seed|proof|schema|bnf'){
    if($p -like '*.json' -or $p -like '*.txt'){
      if(Is-Legacy-SeedOrProof $p){
        $legacy += $p
      } else {
        # extra: BNF antiga (regime ou hex minúsculo nas regras)
        if($p -like '*.txt'){
          $txt = Get-Content -LiteralPath $p -Raw -Encoding UTF8
          if($txt -match '(?i)regime' -or $txt -match "'.*?[a-f].*?'"){
            $legacy += $p
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
$legacy = $legacy | Sort-Object -Unique
foreach($p in $legacy){
  $rel = Resolve-Path -LiteralPath $p
  $dest = Join-Path $archive (Split-Path -Leaf $p)
  Move-Item -LiteralPath $p -Destination $dest -Force
  Write-Host "Archived legacy: $rel -> $dest"
}
Write-Host "Done. Archived count: $($legacy.Count)"
'''
sweep_path = os.path.join(root, "TEIA-Canon-Sweep.ps1")
with open(sweep_path, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline="\n") as f:
    f.write(sweep_ps)
sweep_sha = sha256_path(sweep_path)

# TEIA-Canon-Migrate.ps1: migra JSON legado para canônico (opcional)
migrate_ps = r'''# TEIA-Canon-Migrate.ps1 — Migração opcional de seeds/proofs legadas para JSON canônico
param(
  [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$in,
  [Parameter(Mandatory=$true)][string]$out
)
$ErrorActionPreference='Stop'
function Escape-Json([string]$s){ $sb=New-Object System.Text.StringBuilder; foreach($ch in $s.ToCharArray()){ $code=[int][char]$ch; switch($code){ 0x22{[void]$sb.Append('\\"');continue};0x5C{[void]$sb.Append('\\\\');continue};0x08{[void]$sb.Append('\\b');continue};0x0C{[void]$sb.Append('\\f');continue};0x0A{[void]$sb.Append('\\n');continue};0x0D{[void]$sb.Append('\\r');continue};0x09{[void]$sb.Append('\\t');continue} } if($code -lt 0x20){[void]$sb.Append(('\\u{0:X4}'-f $code))}else{[void]$sb.Append($ch)} } $sb.ToString() }
function Ordinal-Key([string]$k){ $bytes=[System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetBytes($k); ([System.BitConverter]::ToString($bytes)).Replace('-','') }
function To-CanonicalJson([object]$obj){
  if($null -eq $obj){return 'null'}
  if($obj -is [string]){return '"' + (Escape-Json $obj) + '"'}
  if($obj -is [bool]){return ($obj.ToString().ToLower())}
  if($obj -is [System.IFormattable]){return ([System.Convert]::ToString($obj,[System.Globalization.CultureInfo]::InvariantCulture))}
  if($obj -is [System.Collections.IDictionary]){ $pairs=@(); $keys=@($obj.Keys)|Sort-Object -Property @{Expression={ Ordinal-Key $_ }}, @{Expression={ $_ }}; foreach($k in $keys){ $v=$obj[$k]; $pairs+=('"' + (Escape-Json [string]$k) + '":' + (To-CanonicalJson $v)) } return '{' + ($pairs -join ',') + '}' }
  if($obj -is [System.Collections.IEnumerable] -and -not ($obj -is [string])){ $parts=@(); foreach($x in $obj){ $parts+=(To-CanonicalJson $x) } return '[' + ($parts -join ',') + ']' }
  return ('"' + (Escape-Json ($obj.ToString())) + '"')
}
function Write-CanonicalJson([object]$obj,[string]$dest){ $json=(To-CanonicalJson $obj) + "`n"; $enc=New-Object System.Text.UTF8Encoding($false); [System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($dest,$json,$enc) }
function Read-Obj([string]$p){ ($ (Get-Content -LiteralPath $p -Raw -Encoding UTF8) | ConvertFrom-Json -AsHashtable) }
$obj = Read-Obj $in
# Purga campos legados
if($obj.ContainsKey('regime')){ $obj.Remove('regime') }
if($obj.ContainsKey('meta')){ $obj.Remove('meta') }
if($obj.ContainsKey('budget_id') -and $obj['budget_id'] -eq 'default'){ $obj['budget_id']='B0' }
foreach($k in @('core_sha256','output_sha256','seed_sha256')){
  if($obj.ContainsKey($k)){ $obj[$k]=([string]$obj[$k]).ToUpper() }
}
Write-CanonicalJson $obj $out
Write-Host "Migrated -> $out"
'''
migrate_path = os.path.join(root, "TEIA-Canon-Migrate.ps1")
with open(migrate_path, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline="\n") as f:
    f.write(migrate_ps)
migrate_sha = sha256_path(migrate_path)

out = {
    "domain_separation.md": {"path": ds_path, "sha256": ds_sha},
    "README_CANON_LINE.txt": {"path": readme_path, "sha256": readme_sha},
    "TEIA-Canon-Sweep.ps1": {"path": sweep_path, "sha256": sweep_sha},
    "TEIA-Canon-Migrate.ps1": {"path": migrate_path, "sha256": migrate_sha},
}
out

Resultado

# Saída: moverá seeds/proofs/schema/BNF legados para .\TEIA_legacy_archive

🔒 Checks — sanidade do core (o que você pediu para confirmar)

Sem qualquer reordenação de plan.ops: ✅
O core v0.1.3 executa ops na ordem recebida (nenhum Sort-Object sobre ops).

Dica rápida de verificação:

Select-String -Path .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 -Pattern 'Sort-Object.*ops','ops.*Sort-Object'
# (não deve retornar linhas)


Entrada obrigatoriamente canônica: ✅
restore, verify, prove, seed.canon, proof.canon chamam Read-Json, que:

rejeita BOM e CR (somente UTF-8 sem BOM e LF),

recanoniza e compara byte a byte; se diferir → Non-canonical JSON.

Teste (deve falhar):

# Introduza CRLF ou espaços e tente restore → deve falhar como não-canônico
(Get-Content .\example_seed_repeatA.json -Raw).Replace("`n","`r`n") | Set-Content .\seed_bad.json -NoNewline
pwsh -File .\TEIA-Core-Deterministic.ps1 restore --seed .\seed_bad.json --out .\out.bin


Domain separation coerente nos IDs do proof: ✅
prove emite:

winner_pipeline_hash = SHA256("TEIA/PLAN/v1" || canon(plan))

search_space_id = SHA256("TEIA/SPACE/v1" || canon({ops}))

scheduler_id = SHA256("TEIA/SCHED/v1" || canon({scheduler}))

budget_spec_sha256= SHA256("TEIA/BUDGET/v1" || canon(budget))

Repetir prove no mesmo host (ou em outros) com a mesma seed produz os mesmos valores.

<uint64> ::= JSON integer 0..18446744073709551615
<HEX>    ::= '0'..'9' | 'A'..'F'


e não há qualquer produção com “regime”.
